T he  package  includes   a  s et  of  ques tionnaires designed to help gather firs thand information on exis ting programmes  and  policies  in  a  particular  s etting  and  to gauge the commitment and capacity of key institutions and  stakeholders  to  integrate  male  gender  norms  in
